align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2305754"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2305754#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305193" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2305193" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ALakota"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1565541.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ALakota" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Precious-Liquid/Salt-Pepper-80626.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.80626.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Salt & Pepper"title="Salt & Pepper"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2305193ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2305193" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541">ALakota</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-04">10/04/24 18:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Woooo baby. Some gorgeous stuff. Super rich and deep creamy vanilla and a little light citrus that persists for a bit depending on your sensitivity. As a few have said, it has a familiar-feeling dessert or candy flavor going on that I can't quite place, which may be from the orange blossom, praline (never tried), the type of vanilla.. not sure, but if anyone can put their finger on it, it would be interesting to know. Anyway, it is a very appealing flavor, but very creamy and sweet with vanilla right at the heart. This is a cold weather fragrance one hundred percent, obviously. That isn't to say that it is not balanced. There are aromatic and fresh citrus elements in their proper quantities to give the composition some lift. As it develops, there is a deeper masculine musky and woody element, of course, that keeps it from being strictly baked goods. It isn't a fragrance that is remarkably deeper than that, but it smells unique and categorically high quality, and it does what it sets out to do superbly. It is a warm, inviting, and distinctive gourmand masterpiece that, to the right person, might take them on quite the journey into their memories. The only reason I say it might not be blindbuy safe even if you like that idea (I blindbought and I'm in love with it) is because its distinctive flavor might not appeal to certain (perhaps rare) people who are easily sickened by random dessert-esque "allspice-type" aromas. Probably best to sample first unless the cost is not significant to your budget. I don't want that thought to discourage people from trying it, because I might agree that this is the best PDM fragrance for wearing. I own most of them, and I think that it does what it does in its niche better than layton, carlisle, pegasus, or even percival. It is so much more appealing to me than Angel's Share it's not even funny, just for example. It's just a scent that makes sense and is so unchallenging, addictive, appealing, and attractive. Performance would be very difficult for me to determine for several reasons. It is an intimate fragrance for sure, but it is possible that for many people it would have a moderately strong sillage. So far it does not strike me as something that would be prone to low durability. Time will tell, but I have no doubt that this juice will become an insane hit once more people become familiar. Even if you're thinking that you're not really into "gourmands" or sweet fragrances or whatever category, you should try this stuff out. I know the world of fragrance is big, but I think you've come to the right place. AlthaÃ¯r almost transcends its genre, and it's honestly just an amazing smell for a guy of any age over maybe 18. I doubt that five percent of women would object to that statement. <br />
<br />
I wanted to do this original perfume justice, so now that I've made you read War and Peace, I will say this: All of that said, I still  personally prefer Stronger With You Intensely as a sweet cold weather fragrance. I'm sorry, but that composition satisfies my nose on more fronts, is more evocative to me, performs better, and is much, much cheaper than this scent. A grim reality to be certain, but it does not take away from the artistic merit and tangible beauty of this creation. This is only my personal, subjective opinion. <br />
<br />
Edit: I would make an addendum on the performance front. I understand that PDM ain't cheap, and to get what a lot of people are looking for out of a fragrance, it's going to take a few sprays. If you're looking for beast mode and bang per buck, having to spray this six times might sting a little too badly. PDM used to be synonymous with potency in its creations. That may still be the case with a layton or carlisle, but I definitely wouldn't put this near that caliber in terms of strength. I wanna say it's a cuddler unless you're willing to go a little liberal on the sprays. That's going to ding its value proposition, but that's apart from its quality of composition. Just be aware of that if you're not a magical money tree.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2305193"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2305193#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305162" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2305162" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tonileefiore"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/130950"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.130950.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="tonileefiore" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2305162ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2305162" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/130950">tonileefiore</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-04">10/04/24 17:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I recently reignited an interest in locating a unique, well-blended, vanilla-forward fragrance. I am not necessarily searching for an uber-gourmand vanilla fragrance. But I do hope for something warm, enveloping, inviting, comforting.<br />
<br />
Among a few other vanilla-forward fragrances, Sebastian "The Perfume Guy" reviewed PdM Althair and raved about the fragrance. I love Sebastian and I usually find his reviews spot-on. Sebastian and I seem to share loves and likes for very similar perfumes. So, I decided to give this EdP a try.<br />
<br />
Among the several vanilla samples I received, THIS is LOVE. THIS is full-bottle-worthy! This is over-the-top comforting, warm, inviting, unique, just gorgeous!<br />
<br />
WHAT IS that beautiful, lovely, lingering opening note that I keep going back to? It's a note I cannot seem to get enough of!! Perhaps the note is the orange blossom? Or maybe it's the bergamot? It's definitely not cinnamon and it's certainly not cumin. What is that wonderfully pervasive, beautiful floral note that rises beyond every other fragrance note throughout the first 30 minutes, or so after application??<br />
<br />
I think it's orange blossom done in a way I've never experienced it before!!<br />
<br />
And yes, the landing, or base notes are warm vanilla, perfectly balanced elemi, musk, a little almond.  After some time, the perfume lands as a sweet, slightly powdery, slightly woody, slightly gourmand vanilla. But WOW...that opening. I can still smell gentle florals.<br />
<br />
Longevity is okay...for the price of a full bottle, I wish it was better. Silage is minimal.<br />
<br />
I absolutely adore this stuff. Absolutely heavenly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2305162"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2305162#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2304640" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1673973">ethan-fragrantica</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 05:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Althair by Parfums de Marly:<br />
Having tried 4 other PdM fragrances (Layton, Sedley, Greenley and Kalan) I considered the house massively overhyped and underwhelming. The 4 scents I'd tried before were awful to me but this is the opposite. I'm a big fan of Althair. It's like Christmas Day in a bottle. It's performance is great with good projection and longevity and it's a gorgeous sweet, warm, syrupy slightly boozy scent with a spicy opening and a woody base. It is rich and heavy but the bergamot, orange and elemi give it a spark throughout. <br />
<br />
Top notes: Cinnamon, syrup, cardamom, slight citrus<br />
Middle notes: Vanilla, whiskey, elemi resin, gingerbread<br />
Base notes: Woods, ambroxan, vanilla, praline<br />
<br />
Longevity: 4/5<br />
Sillage: 4/5<br />
Scent: 4/5<br />
Design: 5/5<br />
Gender: Masculine<br />
Overall: 4.5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2271065"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2271065#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2269880" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2242786"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2242786#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2238977" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2236885" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="__aer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1847860"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1847860.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="__aer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2236885ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2236885" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1847860">__aer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-02">08/02/24 13:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In many ways, Althair is the typical "modern young male sweet perfume". Synthetic overly sweet vanilla that is reminiscent of bad icecream, some abstract nondescript musky-spicyness in the background, something somewhat edible overlaid (that just adds to the sweetness) and it lasts forever in its screechyness. Althair itself combines that with some resins that are here to stay. Development wise, it doesn't go anywhere. It starts that way and twelve hours later, it's still exactly where it is.<br />
<br />
I've smelled this a hundred times before on random people on the street. I'm sure there's at least five popular current perfumes that smell the same. Probably something in the SWY line, something in the TMW line, and highly likely, a JPG or two. It also reminded me a bit of By The Fireplace after the smoke clears.<br />
<br />
And here's what I don't understand about Althair: While subjectively, the screechy sweetness doesn't do much for me, I can understand that others experience this aspect differently and far more favourable. That's the beauty of perfumery: Different people like different scents. But why spend so much money on a fragrance that can likely be gotten extremely similarly for a third of the asking price of Althair? I would recommend exploring other designer scents and save your money if you like this on yourself. The label alone does not warrant the pricepoint.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2236885"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2236885#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2232285" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2182392">Delicately_unapologetic</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-01">07/01/24 11:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume made me realize that Fragrance community is as toxic as many other communities on the internet.<br />
People hype up PdM for creations like Layton, and Pegasus, but tend to forget that the Maison de Marly mainly focuses on well known ("safe?") DNAs like Sedley, Percival, Darley, but taking a "niche" way with them.<br />
Take those into consideration as you're thinking of an example.<br />
<br />
People say Althair is synthetic, similar to Mercedes Benz CB, and also that it's not something "new" <br />
(more on that later)<br />
The truth is that when I smelled it on me, I was just dumfounded.<br />
<br />
In my honest opinion a huge percentage of the negative reviews either the scent didn't even made it to their nose, or they are just hypebeasts who are just glazing on their favorite youtuber.<br />
The harsh truth is, Althair is a great balanced yet powerful gourmand creation.<br />
With that being said, you really need to try to trace the vanilla, cinnamon, cardamom, praline they come as a complete fuse, then the blossoms in the back so refreshing yet so well balanced.<br />
<br />
To the people that say it feels synthetic, google what Ambroxan is, and then go check how many of your favorite fragrances have it.<br />
<br />
Then to the people that say it smells like Mercedes Benz CB with all due respect, I can see your vision but if you're telling me that if you get blind tested with those 2 titles you wouldn't know the difference? in my opinion you're humiliating yourself.<br />
<br />
People hating on this one because of the reasons I said above, to these guys, please be original, and get informed.<br />
Niche means luxury, and well crafted, not originality nor parthenogenesis.<br />
<br />
Don't ride the hype.<br />
Don't be biased.<br />
Don't you dare get rid of your originality or taste because someone else said it's a bad release.<br />
In the end of the day wear it because you like it.<br />
<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Performance 9/10<br />
<br />
EDIT: I understand if you're not really into such scent profiles to dislike this one.<br />
But no one can deny it's caliber.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2204858"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2204858#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2203023" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; i consider this scent as an artistic expression or effort by someone that tried to replicate pastry, sweets and ice cream as a a realistic scent form that will last a long time on skin or objects, and in no world i want to smell like this nor smell this on people as a their scent around me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2172631">FRAGRANCE_LOVER01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-23">06/23/24 03:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Certainly! Parfums de Marly Althair is a fragrance that embodies sophistication and elegance, making it a standout choice in the world of niche perfumery. Known for its luxurious blends and distinctive compositions, Parfums de Marly has carved out a niche for itself among fragrance enthusiasts who appreciate fine craftsmanship and unique olfactory experiences. Althair, in particular, showcases the brand's commitment to quality and artistry, offering a scent that is both complex and captivating.<br />
<br />
At its heart, Althair is characterized by a rich and aromatic profile that combines spicy and woody notes with a hint of sweetness. The fragrance opens with a burst of freshness, featuring vibrant citrus notes that immediately invigorate the senses. This initial brightness is complemented by the warmth of spices such as cardamom and nutmeg, which add depth and complexity to the composition. These spicy elements create a dynamic contrast against the citrus, establishing a compelling aromatic journey from the first spray.<br />
<br />
As Althair develops on the skin, the heart notes reveal themselves with a blend of aromatic lavender and herbal sage. These herbal accents contribute a refined and slightly medicinal quality to the fragrance, adding an intriguing twist to the overall composition. The herbal notes are balanced by the subtle sweetness of tonka bean, which emerges in the mid-phase, imparting a creamy and comforting aspect to the scent.<br />
<br />
One of the most distinctive features of Althair is its sophisticated base, which is anchored by rich and resinous amber. The amber accord in Althair is deep and opulent, providing a luxurious foundation that enhances the longevity and sillage of the fragrance. This amber base is further enriched by the smooth and creamy nuances of vanilla, which lend a soft and sensual touch to the dry-down. Together, these base notes create a lasting impression that is both memorable and irresistible.<br />
<br />
In terms of performance, Althair is renowned for its longevity and projection. It has a robust presence that allows it to linger on the skin throughout the day, making it well-suited for both daytime wear and evening occasions. The fragrance evolves gracefully over time, revealing different facets of its complex composition as it interacts with the wearer's skin chemistry.<br />
<br />
Beyond its olfactory appeal, Althair is housed in Parfums de Marly's signature bottle, which reflects the brand's commitment to luxury and refinement. The bottle features a regal design with a heavy glass base and a decorative cap adorned with the brand's crest. This attention to detail extends to every aspect of the fragrance experience, from the presentation to the scent itself, ensuring that Althair embodies the essence of luxury and sophistication.<br />
<br />
In conclusion, Parfums de Marly Althair stands out as a masterpiece within the brand's impressive lineup of fragrances. It captivates with its complex blend of citrus, spices, herbs, and rich amber, offering a sensory journey that is both refined and memorable. Whether you are a connoisseur of niche fragrances or someone looking to explore new olfactory horizons, Althair represents a compelling choice that embodies the artistry and craftsmanship synonymous with Parfums de Marly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Parfume d'E marley Althair is a fragrance that encapsulates the essence of sophistication and luxury. From the moment I first experienced its captivating aroma, I was transported to a world of opulence and grace. This outstanding fragrance is a true masterpiece that deserves to be celebrated.<br />
<br />
<br />
At the heart of Parfume d'E marley Althair lies a harmonious blend of notes that dance gracefully together, creating a symphony of olfactory delight. The fragrance opens with a burst of citrusy bergamot, which instantly invigorates the senses and sets the stage for the journey ahead. As the scent develops, the intoxicating floral notes of jasmine and rose take center stage, adding a touch of elegance and femininity. Finally, the warm and sensual base notes of sandalwood and vanilla provide a comforting and alluring embrace that lingers on the skin.<br />
<br />
Accords:<br />
The accords in Parfume d'E marley Althair are nothing short of breathtaking. The fragrance seamlessly weaves together contrasting elements to create a harmonious balance. The floral accords are vibrant and radiant, while the woody accords add depth and sophistication. There is a delicate interplay between the fresh and the warm, the light and the dark, resulting in a fragrance that is both captivating and intriguing.<br />
<br />
Longevity:<br />
One of the most impressive aspects of Parfume d'Emarley Althair is its remarkable longevity. This fragrance has the power to stay with you throughout the day, enveloping you in its enchanting aura from morning until night. The carefully crafted composition ensures that the scent remains vibrant and true, allowing you to enjoy its beauty for hours on end. It is truly a testament to the quality and craftsmanship of Parfume d'Emarley.<br />
<br />
Parfume d'Emarley Althair is a fragrance that leaves a lasting impression. From its exquisite notes to its captivating accords and long-lasting presence, it is a true gem in the world of perfumery. Whether you are seeking a scent for a special occasion or simply want to indulge in a touch of luxury, Althair is a fragrance that will never disappoint. Prepare to be embraced by its elegance and sophistication, and let it transport you to a world of timeless beauty.<br />
<br />

The first time I smelled AlthaÃ¯r, I really didn't like it at all. It wasn't hate, but almost. The second time was the same. I can't explain why, but I have a tendency not to like gourmand perfumes. I find them too dense, not very versatile, and some are cloying. The third time I tried my sample of AlthaÃ¯r was different. I went from really disliking it to loving this perfume! I have never smelled Mercedes Club Black, but of all the vanilla fragrances I have tried, this one doesn't resemble anything I know. Itâs different. It has a kind of freshness that I appreciate in perfumes of this "family" (I place it at the opposite end, without any freshness, to perfumes like Angelâs Share, Stronger With You Intensely, Oajan, etc.), and I use this fragrance on days with temperatures in the low twenties Celsius without any problem (I am very considerate of those around me and I commute daily by train to my job), just like I use Tom Ford's Noir Extreme Parfum, for example.<br />
<br />
In terms of longevity and projection, this PDM is slightly below the other perfumes from the brand that I have and/or have tried, but even so, I think it is worth buying this perfume (never in "blind buy mode," of course) because it lasts between 7 and 9 hours with moderate projection (which I appreciate).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1544521">0xrafae</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-15">06/15/24 00:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The sugar levels in this PdM are surprisingly toned down, though they're still pretty strong compared to other brands. This reduced sweetness and a dense, milky vibe make Althair rather pleasant. It's a good choice if you enjoy caramel and don't mind the price. Personally, that's not me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2188802"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2188802#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2188553" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2188553" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Aromaventure"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2152922"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2152922.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Aromaventure" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2188553ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2188553" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2152922">Aromaventure</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-14">06/14/24 17:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Review: AlthaÃ¯r by Parfums de Marly<br />
Fragrance Name: AlthaÃ¯r<br />
Brand: Parfums de Marly<br />
Release Year: 2021<br />
Perfumer: Hamid Merati-Kashani<br />
<br />
Introduction<br />
Parfums de Marly, a brand renowned for its luxurious and historically inspired fragrances, introduces AlthaÃ¯r, a scent that masterfully combines oriental and gourmand elements. As with many creations from Parfums de Marly, AlthaÃ¯r is a testament to the brand's dedication to elegance, sophistication, and high-quality ingredients.<br />
<br />
Scent Profile<br />
Top Notes: Bergamot, Mandarin Orange<br />
Heart Notes: Almond, Cinnamon, Jasmine<br />
Base Notes: Vanilla, Amber, Sandalwood, Musk<br />
<br />
Upon the initial spray, AlthaÃ¯r greets you with a bright and invigorating burst of bergamot and mandarin orange. The citrusy opening is fresh and welcoming, setting the stage for the rich and complex heart notes that follow.<br />
<br />
As the fragrance develops, the heart reveals a harmonious blend of almond and cinnamon, accompanied by a subtle hint of jasmine. The almond note adds a creamy, slightly nutty dimension, while the cinnamon introduces a warm, spicy facet. The jasmine provides a delicate floral touch, balancing the richness of the heart notes.<br />
<br />
The base of AlthaÃ¯r is where the fragrance truly shines and lingers. Vanilla and amber form a sweet, resinous foundation, enveloped by the creamy smoothness of sandalwood and the warmth of musk. This combination creates a lasting impression that is both comforting and sensual, making AlthaÃ¯r an ideal choice for evening wear and special occasions.<br />
<br />
Performance<br />
AlthaÃ¯r boasts impressive longevity and sillage. It is a fragrance that remains noticeable throughout the day, requiring only a minimal reapplication to maintain its presence. The projection is moderate, ensuring that while the scent is discernible, it is never overpowering.<br />
<br />
Versatility<br />
While AlthaÃ¯r is versatile enough for various occasions, its opulent and warm profile makes it particularly well-suited for cooler weather and evening events. The gourmand and oriental notes provide a comforting yet sophisticated aura, perfect for intimate gatherings or formal settings.<br />
<br />
Presentation<br />
In typical Parfums de Marly fashion, AlthaÃ¯r is presented in a beautifully crafted bottle that exudes luxury. The elegant design, featuring a solid, weighty bottle with intricate detailing, mirrors the refined nature of the fragrance within.<br />
<br />
Conclusion<br />
AlthaÃ¯r by Parfums de Marly is a captivating addition to any fragrance collection. Its masterful blend of citrus, spice, and gourmand notes creates a scent that is both alluring and memorable. For those seeking a fragrance that balances opulence with subtlety, AlthaÃ¯r is an exceptional choice.<br />
<br />
Rating: 9/10<br />
<br />
Pros:<br />
<br />
  Rich and complex scent profile<br />
  Excellent longevity and moderate sillage<br />
  Luxurious presentation<br />
<br />
Cons:<br />
<br />
  Best suited for cooler weather and evenings, which may limit year-round versatility<br />
<br />
AlthaÃ¯r stands as a testament to Parfums de Marly's expertise in crafting high-quality, sophisticated fragrances that leave a lasting impression.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; When it first released I fell in love with Altairâs scent, and now I finally got it. Althair is basically Layton and Oajan mixed togethor. You get that beautiful cardamon, cinnamon, gourmand esc start alongside the more fresh bergamot note. Then the vanilla in the middle note helps to give a more edible feel to this scent. Then the woodiness off the base note gives this a masculine touch. <br />
<br />
Althair lasts around 9-10 hours, and projects quite well. Itâs a scent to wear for the winter and fall. Itâs a great scent to wear in all occasions. A perfect date night fragrance due to its gourmand smell. <br />
<br />
Althair does cost an around 400 dollars, and at that price I feel like a significantly better alternative which gives the best gourmand smell is angel share. But I still do think Althair is a good purchase, and is a top 3 de Marley fragrance.<br />
<br />
Scent: 10<br />
Projection: 8<br />
Longevity: 9<br />
Value: 8<br />

It smells great, it'll be mass pleasing, but it lacks an artistic touch. It's just a very great sweet perfume, but from a niche house with such a high price tag, I really wanted more. Unisex leaning masculine.<br />

Performance is massive on my skin, 12+ hours longevity with big sillage. Will try again as I got a sample, the first hour or so is very unisex, but I find the dry down way more masculine. <br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2170403" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jbozz"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1445544"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1445544.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jbozz" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.94983.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="MYSLF Le Parfum"title="MYSLF Le Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2170403ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2170403" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1445544">jbozz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-28">05/28/24 11:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really shouldn't judge and review fragrances based on first impressions. That's what I did with this one, basically writing it off as simplistic (which it kinda is), but now here I am having mostly eaten my words and just ordered a full bottle. It does follow the usual PDM pattern of taking a designer-like scent profile and refining it on a niche level, and Althair is no exception. But the brilliance of this fragrance is not just the blending and high quality ingredients, but its versatilty. Most vanilla-forward men's fragrances are heavy, thick and cloying in anything but cold temps, but the perfumer managed to give this one a really nice freshness while retaining that beautiful vanilla sweetness so you could wear this in almost any weather except high heat. It's gourmand to the extent you wanna eat it (like a sexy French vanilla ice cream) but still fresh enough to wear as a daily signature scent if you wish without it being "too much". How this balance was achieved is kind of genius really, and Althair deserves any and all praise it gets. It's much better than you may initially think it to be and I look forward to wearing this superb creation.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2170403"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2170403#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2169831" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; My PDM's are by far my most complemented fragrances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2136738"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2136738#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2136479" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Sparkly candy sweet vanilla, has an effervesce that hits you before you get a gourmand cinnamon that gives a depth to the opening. After two hours it dries down to a very long lasting intimate vanilla scent. All of that being said, I wore it twice, it's collecting dust. It can't compete with Babycat, and while it does compete with MB CB, competing with a $40 cheapie isn't exactly a brag.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2127256"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2127256#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2124044" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2182392">Delicately_unapologetic</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-01">07/01/24 11:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume made me realize that Fragrance community is as toxic as many other communities on the internet.<br />
People hype up PdM for creations like Layton, and Pegasus, but tend to forget that the Maison de Marly mainly focuses on well known ("safe?") DNAs like Sedley, Percival, Darley, but taking a "niche" way with them.<br />
Take those into consideration as you're thinking of an example.<br />
<br />
People say Althair is synthetic, similar to Mercedes Benz CB, and also that it's not something "new" <br />
(more on that later)<br />
The truth is that when I smelled it on me, I was just dumfounded.<br />
<br />
In my honest opinion a huge percentage of the negative reviews either the scent didn't even made it to their nose, or they are just hypebeasts who are just glazing on their favorite youtuber.<br />
The harsh truth is, Althair is a great balanced yet powerful gourmand creation.<br />
With that being said, you really need to try to trace the vanilla, cinnamon, cardamom, praline they come as a complete fuse, then the blossoms in the back so refreshing yet so well balanced.<br />
<br />
To the people that say it feels synthetic, google what Ambroxan is, and then go check how many of your favorite fragrances have it.<br />
<br />
Then to the people that say it smells like Mercedes Benz CB with all due respect, I can see your vision but if you're telling me that if you get blind tested with those 2 titles you wouldn't know the difference? in my opinion you're humiliating yourself.<br />
<br />
People hating on this one because of the reasons I said above, to these guys, please be original, and get informed.<br />
Niche means luxury, and well crafted, not originality nor parthenogenesis.<br />
<br />
Don't ride the hype.<br />
Don't be biased.<br />
Don't you dare get rid of your originality or taste because someone else said it's a bad release.<br />
In the end of the day wear it because you like it.<br />
<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Performance 9/10<br />
<br />
EDIT: I understand if you're not really into such scent profiles to dislike this one.<br />
But no one can deny it's caliber.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2204858"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2204858#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1918666" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1503389">mizur</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-21">03/21/24 15:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I know I will get bashed by fan boys and paid reviewers from PDM, but I have to tell the truth about this fragrance.<br />
<br />
Let me start by saying that I really love the smell of AlthaÃ¯r, and that going on scent alone, itâs quite a unique combination, probably the best sweet/aromatic perfume I have ever smelled.<br />
<br />
So, if you think of perfumes solely based on how they smell, and you like sweet perfumes, then AlthaÃ¯r is a must for youâ¦ I just wish life was still that easy for meâ¦<br />
<br />
In my head I evaluate a lot of characteristics beyond how a perfume smellsâ¦ obviously, if I donât like the scent that would be the end of itâ¦ but if I do like it, a whole process (small, but process) starts in my head before deciding if I should purchase such fragrance.<br />
<br />
Still, I  have to be honest, regardless of the final score in my head, I will most likely end up buying every perfume that I like, but thatâs because my collectorâs (OCD) side takes overâ¦ but people in general shouldnât do thatâ¦ people should really pay attention to what their buying, perfumes are not cheap, specially niche perfumes, and many are truly garbage. That is why Fragrantica is such a life saverâ¦ people should really read reviews before making a purchase, and they should specifically focus on bad and intermediate reviewsâ¦ sadly, the good reviews left on very famous perfumes are usually wrong or fake.<br />
<br />
But I digress, letâs get into this juiceâ¦<br />
<br />
Iâve already said it, it smells amazingâ¦ and it is âuniqueââ¦ but only because itâs a unique mixture of several other great perfumes with delicious accordsâ¦ for starters, the main envelope is from Le Male, Pegasus, Reflection (and many others), the secondary envelope is within the realm of The Most Wanted line, just with an orange accord instead of a grape one, and finally, on top of the previous two they added a lovely and delicious vanilla/caramel scent, scent that you can find in a myriad of perfumes, including a few by Zara.<br />
<br />
So yes, AlthaÃ¯r smells amazingâ¦ but a three part layering of way cheaper perfumes, some of which you might already have, will bring you the exact same scent.<br />
<br />
Now, letâs delve into performance, sillage and projection are non-existent, this perfume is intimate from the start, quite present but intimate, with longevity not being that great either, after just a couple of hours since I oversprayed it was still noticeable but very very faint, it remained like that for about 6 more hours until it completely disappeared around the 8th hour. Itâs important to mention that to achieve such a result I oversprayed myself and my clothes.<br />
<br />
A few months ago I spoke with Yvan Jaqueline regarding the longevity (or lack thereof) of PDM perfumes, and his explanation was that their natural ingredients are of so high quality that they breakup very fast against certain types of body chemistryâ¦ but come on, this perfume has ambroxan which is nowhere near natural, and still, it blows away like the windâ¦ in reality, itâs their perfumeâs concentration which is at fault.<br />
<br />
And no matter what other reviewers, past or future, have said or will say, this perfume is NOT a beast, nor it last past a few hours.<br />
<br />
So, the conclusion in my head, after my small process, is that itâs not worth the purchaseâ¦ obviously, being myself, I still purchased it.<br />
<br />
But for anyone else reading this review, you can get any Le Male clone, plus any from the The Most Wanted line, and finally, any vanilla/caramel perfume from Zara, and layer the threeâ¦ you will spend half as much, smell the same, and it will probably last longer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="84109"comment_id="2099892"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Althair-84109.html?ccid=2099892#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="84109" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
